<div class="para">吕吉人<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />旅美华裔画家<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />他幼时就酷爱画画<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />青少年时拜国画大师贺子健为师<img class="pchar" />立志用毛笔<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />宣纸作画<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" <div class="para">由<a target=_blank href="/view/65179.htm">陈香梅</a>女士<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=627490465706796950862818540" />陈香梅教育基金会董事长<img class="pchar" <div class="para">其中高2.20米<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />长10.56米<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />画面达210多平方尺<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />描写新上海黄浦江两岸的夜景的<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=108932030168486474428289659" />浦江灿烂图<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=881584074518235945079112911" />这幅作品就是作者在惊叹上海发展如此迅速的心情下创作出来的<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />在画这幅作品的二十多年前他去美国<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />当时他就在黄浦江旁边的一幢大楼里上班<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />隔着窗户能看见对岸的景象<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />那时的浦江两岸反差强烈<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />一边是万国建筑和人潮涌动的街巷<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />一边则是成片的工厂<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />低矮的农舍和宽阔的农田<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />但浦江两岸天翻地覆的巨变着实令人震撼<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />1999年他在<a target=_blank href="/view/368002.htm">上海国际会议中心</a>创作了这幅作品<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>

<div class="para">吕吉人虽然定居美国<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />但他是一位受过传统教育和有现代思维的中国<a target=_blank href="/view/67095.htm">艺术家</a><img href="/view/1689.htm">毛泽东</a>像章珍藏馆内收藏了由金山区私人收藏家缪时方先生多年收藏的近3000枚各式各样的毛主席像章<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />珍藏馆不仅集中展出了各地以及各大军区<img <div class="para">白牛转世顺乎天</div>
<div class="para">三百园里忠烈在</div>
<div class="para">施王庙中供神仙<br/>　　古戏台前听新曲</div>
<div class="para">清风桥畔缅圣贤<br/>　　穷尽脑汁难为句<br/>　　只叹如此好人间</div>
